The app reads a larger offline file that you can download to your device's storage (e.g. microSD card or other drive). Offline files are available for Wikipedia, Wiktionary, Wikivoyage, Wikimedicine, Wikimaths, TED Talks, Project Gutenberg, etc., in all the available Wikipedia languages.\r\n\r\nIf you just want Wikivoyage (Offline Travel Guide) or WikiMed (Medical Wikipedia) in English, we have two sister apps in this Store that come completely pre-packaged (no extra download required): search for \"Wikivoyage by Kiwix\" or for \"WikiMed\" for further details.\r\n\r\nOffline files are called ZIM Archives.
